[Starfire II] and [Starfire III] have even stronger buff effects.

尋獵者=Hunter
{{A}}初始狀態，能夠為敵人添加、結算、刷新『流血』狀態。『流血』：每回合受到基於自身最大生命值的萬能屬性傷害與{{A}}攻擊力的物理屬性傷害。=Your initial state, can add, trigger, and refresh [Bleed]. [Bleed]: Take Almighty damage based on the target's Max HP and Phys damage based on Messa's ATK each turn.

<color\=#66ccff>『行刑官』</color>=<color\=#66ccff>[Executioner]</color>
行刑官=Executioner
{{A}}使用『夜幕已至』後轉變為『行刑官』狀態，技能模式發生改變，能夠清除敵人的『流血』層數並額外造成『撕裂』傷害。『撕裂』：基於目標『流血』層數造成的額外傷害。=Transform to [Executioner] after using [Night's Arrival], changing skills, can remove [Bleed] to deal [Laceration] damage. [Laceration]: Deal damage based on [Bleed] stacks.

聖歌=Holy Song
{{A}}的特殊戰鬥資源，用於提升『貫穿時空的輪轉』的技能效果與減少釋放『華光下的治癒詩』後所需的準備時間。={{A}}'s special resource, used to increase the skill effect of [Wheel of Time] and decrease [Poem of Radiance] preparation time.
<color\=#66ccff>總傷害增幅</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Total DMG Bonus</color>
所有傷害的最終增幅效果，此效果為獨立加成。=Increase the Final DMG of all damage, this is an independent bonus.
